# Caret notation character escape sequences

\c(		)syntax-error(	\c(	"Unterminated group"

# RegExp modifiers ((?ims-ims:pattern))

## Basic ignoreCase modifier
(?i:abc)		(?i:abc)	ABC	[{"captures":["ABC"],"index":0}]
(?i:abc)		(?i:abc)	abc	[{"captures":["abc"],"index":0}]
(?i:abc)		(?i:abc)	AbC	[{"captures":["AbC"],"index":0}]
(?i:abc)	u	(?i:abc)	ABC	[{"captures":["ABC"],"index":0}]
(?i:abc)	u	(?i:abc)	abc	[{"captures":["abc"],"index":0}]

## Basic multiline modifier
(?m:^a)		"(?:(?<=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|^)a)"	"b\na"	[{"captures":["a"],"index":2}]
(?m:a$)		"(?:a(?=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|$))"	"a\nb"	[{"captures":["a"],"index":0}]
(?m:^a$)		"(?:(?<=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|^)a(?=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|$))"	"b\na\nb"	[{"captures":["a"],"index":2}]

## Basic dotAll modifier
(?s:.)		"(?:[\\s\\S])"	"\n"	[{"captures":["\n"],"index":0}]
(?s:.)		"(?:[\\s\\S])"	a	[{"captures":["a"],"index":0}]
(?s:.)		"(?:[\\s\\S])"	"\r"	[{"captures":["\r"],"index":0}]

## Remove modifiers
(?-i:abc)	i	(?-i:abc)	abc	[{"captures":["abc"],"index":0}]
(?-i:abc)	i	(?-i:abc)	ABC	[]
(?-s:.)	s	"(?:[^\n\r\u2028\u2029])"	a	[{"captures":["a"],"index":0}]
(?-s:.)	s	"(?:[^\n\r\u2028\u2029])"	"\n"	[]
(?-m:^a)	m	(?:^a)	"b\na"	[]
(?-m:^a)	m	(?:^a)	a	[{"captures":["a"],"index":0}]

## Combined add modifiers
(?im:^abc)		"(?i:(?<=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|^)abc)"	"b\nabc"	[{"captures":["abc"],"index":2}]
(?im:^abc)		"(?i:(?<=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|^)abc)"	"b\nABC"	[{"captures":["ABC"],"index":2}]
(?is:.abc)		"(?i:[\\s\\S]abc)"	"\nabc"	[{"captures":["\nabc"],"index":0}]
(?is:.abc)		"(?i:[\\s\\S]abc)"	"\nABC"	[{"captures":["\nABC"],"index":0}]
(?ims:^.a)		"(?i:(?<=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|^)[\\s\\S]a)"	"b\n\na"	[{"captures":["\na"],"index":2}]

## Add + remove modifiers
(?i-m:^abc)	m	(?i:^abc)	abc	[{"captures":["abc"],"index":0}]
(?i-m:^abc)	m	(?i:^abc)	ABC	[{"captures":["ABC"],"index":0}]
(?i-m:^abc)	m	(?i:^abc)	"b\nabc"	[]
(?m-i:^abc)	i	"(?-i:(?<=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|^)abc)"	"b\nabc"	[{"captures":["abc"],"index":2}]
(?m-i:^abc)	i	"(?-i:(?<=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|^)abc)"	"b\nABC"	[]

## Empty remove syntax
(?s-:.)		"(?:[\\s\\S])"	"\n"	[{"captures":["\n"],"index":0}]
(?s-:.)		"(?:[\\s\\S])"	a	[{"captures":["a"],"index":0}]
(?m-:^a)		"(?:(?<=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|^)a)"	"b\na"	[{"captures":["a"],"index":2}]

## Scoping вАФ modifier only applies inside group
a(?i:b)c		a(?i:b)c	aBc	[{"captures":["aBc"],"index":0}]
a(?i:b)c		a(?i:b)c	ABc	[]
a(?i:b)c		a(?i:b)c	aBC	[]
a(?i:b)c		a(?i:b)c	abc	[{"captures":["abc"],"index":0}]

## Nested modifier groups
(?s:(?-s:.).)		"(?:(?:[^\n\r\u2028\u2029])[\\s\\S])"	"a\n"	[{"captures":["a\n"],"index":0}]
(?s:(?-s:.).)		"(?:(?:[^\n\r\u2028\u2029])[\\s\\S])"	"\n\n"	[]
(?i:(?-i:a)b)		(?i:(?-i:a)b)	aB	[{"captures":["aB"],"index":0}]
(?i:(?-i:a)b)		(?i:(?-i:a)b)	AB	[]
(?i:(?-i:a)b)		(?i:(?-i:a)b)	ab	[{"captures":["ab"],"index":0}]

## Quantifier after modifier group
(?i:a)+		(?i:a)+	aAaA	[{"captures":["aAaA"],"index":0}]
(?s:.){2}		"(?:[\\s\\S]){2}"	"a\n"	[{"captures":["a\n"],"index":0}]
(?i:a)*		(?i:a)*	aA	[{"captures":["aA"],"index":0},{"captures":[""],"index":2}]

## Alternation inside modifier group
(?i:a|B)		(?i:a|B)	a	[{"captures":["a"],"index":0}]
(?i:a|B)		(?i:a|B)	b	[{"captures":["b"],"index":0}]
(?i:a|B)		(?i:a|B)	A	[{"captures":["A"],"index":0}]
(?i:a|B)		(?i:a|B)	B	[{"captures":["B"],"index":0}]

## Capturing group inside modifier group
(?i:(a)b)		(?i:(a)b)	AB	[{"captures":["AB","A"],"index":0}]

# With u flag
(?i:abc)	u	(?i:abc)	AbC	[{"captures":["AbC"],"index":0}]
(?s:.)	u	"(?:(?:[\ud800-\udbff][\udc00-\udfff]|[\ud800-\udbff](?![\udc00-\udfff])|(?<![\ud800-\udbff])[\udc00-\udfff]|[^\ud800-\udfff]))"	"\n"	[{"captures":["\n"],"index":0}]
(?m:^a)	u	"(?:(?<=[\n\r\u2028\u2029]|^)a)"	"b\na"	[{"captures":["a"],"index":2}]

## Error cases (these should produce syntax errors)
(?z:a)		)syntax-error(	a	"Invalid group"
(?ii:a)		)syntax-error(	a	"Repeated flag in flag group"
(?i-i:a)		)syntax-error(	a	"Repeated flag in flag group"
(?i-s-i:a)		)syntax-error(	a	"Multiple dashes in flag group"
(?-:a)		)syntax-error(	a	"Invalid flag group"
(?I:a)		)syntax-error(	a	"Invalid group"
(?1:a)		)syntax-error(	a	"Invalid group"
(?-ss:a)		)syntax-error(	a	"Repeated flag in flag group"
(?mm:a)		)syntax-error(	a	"Repeated flag in flag group"

## Sequential modifier groups
(?i:a)(?s:.)		"(?i:a)(?:[\\s\\S])"	"A\n"	[{"captures":["A\n"],"index":0}]
(?i:a)b		(?i:a)b	Ab	[{"captures":["Ab"],"index":0}]

## Empty content modifier groups
(?i:)		(?i:)	a	[{"captures":[""],"index":0},{"captures":[""],"index":1}]
(?s:)		(?:)	a	[{"captures":[""],"index":0},{"captures":[""],"index":1}]
(?m:)		(?:)	a	[{"captures":[""],"index":0},{"captures":[""],"index":1}]
